[30;1m573 | [0m[35m### Broadcast[0m
[30;1m574 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m575 | [0m[35mSome c2cwsgiutils APIs effect or query the state of the WSGI server. Since only one process out of t[0m
[30;1m576 | [0m[35m(by default) time the number of servers gets a query, only this one will be affected. To avoid that,[0m
[30;1m577 | [0m[35mcan configure c2cwsgiutils to use Redis pub/sub to broadcast those requests and collect the answers.[0m
[30;1m578 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m579 | [0m[35mThe impacted APIs are:[0m

[30;1m459 | [0m[35m- \>=2: Use those at your convenience. Pingdom and CO are usually setup at max_level=100. So stay be[0m

[30;1m641 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m644 | [0m[35mcan configure c2cwsgiutils to use Redis pub/sub to broadcast those requests and collect the answers.[0m
[30;1m645 | [0m[35m[0m
